           - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
         
         ## 4. Data Storage
         
         The 'BookstoreOnline' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:
         
         ### 1. Books Data
         - **File Name**: `books.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
           2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
           3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
           ```
         
         ### 2. Categories Data
         - **File Name**: `categories.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           category_id|category_name|description
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
           2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
           3|Science|Scientific topics and research
           ```
         
         ### 3. Cart Data
         - **File Name**: `cart.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|1|2|2025-01-15
           2|3|1|2025-01-16
           ```
         
         ### 4. Orders Data
         - **File Name**: `orders.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
           2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
           ```
         
         ### 5. Order Items Data
         - **File Name**: `order_items.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|1|1|2|12.99
           2|1|3|1|14.99
           3|2|2|1|16.99
           ```
         
         ### 6. Reviews Data
         - **File Name**: `reviews.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
           2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
           3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
           ```
         
         ### 7. Bestsellers Data
         - **File Name**: `bestsellers.txt`
         - **Data Format**:
           ```
           book_id|sales_count|period
           ```
         - **Example Data**:
           ```
           2|150|This Month
           1|120|This Month
           3|95|This Month
           ```

         === design_spec.md ===
         # BookstoreOnline Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         ### 1. Dashboard
         - Route Path: `/`
         - Function Name: `dashboard`
         - HTTP Methods: GET
         - Template Rendered: `dashboard.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `featured_books` (List[Dict]): List of featured books with keys `book_id`, `title`, `author`, `price`.
         - POST Behavior: None
         
         ### 2. Book Catalog
         - Route Path: `/catalog`
         - Function Name: `book_catalog`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `catalog.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `books` (List[Dict]): List of books filtered/searched.
           - `categories` (List[Dict]): List of available categories.
           - `selected_category` (str|None): Currently selected category ID or None.
           - `search_query` (str): Current search string.
         - POST Behavior: Handles search and filter submissions, updates displayed books accordingly.
         
         ### 3. Book Details
         - Route Path: `/book/<int:book_id>`
         - Function Name: `book_details`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `details.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` (Dict): Book details.
           - `reviews` (List[Dict]): Related customer reviews for the book.
         - POST Behavior: Allows adding book to cart triggered by button `add-to-cart-button`.
         
         ### 4. Shopping Cart
         - Route Path: `/cart`
         - Function Name: `shopping_cart`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `cart.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `cart_items` (List[Dict]): Cart items, each with `item_id`, `book_id`, `title`, `quantity`, `price`, and `subtotal`.
           - `total_amount` (float): Total cart price.
         - POST Behavior: Handles updates to item quantity via input IDs `update-quantity-{item_id}` and removal of items via buttons `remove-item-button-{item_id}`.
         
         ### 5. Checkout
         - Route Path: `/checkout`
         - Function Name: `checkout`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `checkout.html`
         - Context Variables: None
         - POST Behavior: Processes submitted customer name, shipping address, and payment method via form with `place-order-button`.
         
         ### 6. Order History
         - Route Path: `/orders`
         - Function Name: `order_history`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `history.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `orders` (List[Dict]): List of customer orders.
           - `status_filter` (str): Current status filter (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).
         - POST Behavior: Filtering by order status and viewing order details triggered by button `view-order-button-{order_id}`.
         
         ### 7. Reviews
         - Route Path: `/reviews`
         - Function Name: `reviews`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `reviews.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `reviews` (List[Dict]): Customer reviews.
           - `rating_filter` (str|int): Star rating filter selected.
         - POST Behavior: Filter reviews by rating dropdown, navigate to write review via `write-review-button`.
         
         ### 8. Write Review
         - Route Path: `/write_review`
         - Function Name: `write_review`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `write_review.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `purchased_books` (List[Dict]): Books eligible for reviews.
         - POST Behavior: Review submission handling with fields `select-book`, `rating-select`, `review-text` and `submit-review-button`.
         
         ### 9. Bestsellers
         - Route Path: `/bestsellers`
         - Function Name: `bestsellers`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `bestsellers.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `bestsellers` (List[Dict]): List of bestselling books.
           - `time_period` (str): Selected time period filter.
         - POST Behavior: Handles time period filter and book detail views.
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### dashboard.html
         - File path: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page title: "Bookstore Dashboard"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Bookstore Dashboard</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div): Main container
           - `featured-books` (Div): Displays featured books
           - `browse-catalog-button` (Button): Navigates to `/catalog`
           - `view-cart-button` (Button): Navigates to `/cart`
           - `bestsellers-button` (Button): Navigates to `/bestsellers`
         - Context variables: `featured_books`
         - Navigation via `url_for` calls to respective routes
         - No forms
         
         ### catalog.html
         - File path: `templates/catalog.html`
         - Page title: "Book Catalog"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Book Catalog</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `catalog-page` (Div): Main container
           - `search-input` (Input): Text search input
           - `category-filter` (Dropdown): Category filter
           - `books-grid` (Div): Container for book cards
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): View book details button per book
         - Context variables: `books`, `categories`, `selected_category`, `search_query`
         - Buttons navigation via `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`
         - Search and filter via POST form submission
         
         ### details.html
         - File path: `templates/details.html`
         - Page title: "Book Details"
         - Main heading: `<h1 id="book-title">{{ book.title }}</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `book-details-page` (Div): Container
           - `book-author` (Div): Book author
           - `book-price` (Div): Book price
           - `add-to-cart-button` (Button): Adds book to cart (POST button)
           - `book-reviews` (Div): Displays reviews
         - Context variables: `book`, `reviews`
         - POST form with `add-to-cart-button` to add the book to the cart
         
         ### cart.html
         - File path: `templates/cart.html`
         - Page title: "Shopping Cart"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Shopping Cart</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `cart-page` (Div): Main container
           - `cart-items-table` (Table): Displays cart items
           - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input Number): Quantity input for each cart item
           - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button): Button to remove item from cart
           - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button): Proceeds to checkout
           - `total-amount` (Div): Displays total amount
         - Context variables: `cart_items`, `total_amount`
         - POST forms for quantity update and removal
         
         ### checkout.html
         - File path: `templates/checkout.html`
         - Page title: "Checkout"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Checkout</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `checkout-page` (Div): Container
           - `customer-name` (Input): Customer name input
           - `shipping-address` (Textarea): Shipping address input
           - `payment-method` (Dropdown): Payment method selection
           - `place-order-button` (Button): Submit order
         - Context variables: None
         - POST form submission
         
         ### history.html
         - File path: `templates/history.html`
         - Page title: "Order History"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Order History</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `orders-page` (Div): Container
           - `orders-table` (Table): Table listing order records
           - `view-order-button-{order_id}` (Button): View order details
           - `order-status-filter` (Dropdown): Filter orders by status
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context variables: `orders`, `status_filter`
         - POST form to filter or view order
         
         ### reviews.html
         - File path: `templates/reviews.html`
         - Page title: "Customer Reviews"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Customer Reviews</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `reviews-page` (Div): Container
           - `reviews-list` (Div): Contains all reviews
           - `write-review-button` (Button): Navigate to write review page
           - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown): Filter reviews by rating
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context variables: `reviews`, `rating_filter`
         - POST form submission
         
         ### write_review.html
         - File path: `templates/write_review.html`
         - Page title: "Write a Review"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Write a Review</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `write-review-page` (Div): Container
           - `select-book` (Dropdown): Select book to review
           - `rating-select` (Dropdown): Select rating 1-5
           - `review-text` (Textarea): Input review text
           - `submit-review-button` (Button): Submit review
         - Context variables: `purchased_books`
         - POST form submission
         
         ### bestsellers.html
         - File path: `templates/bestsellers.html`
         - Page title: "Bestsellers"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Bestsellers</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `bestsellers-page` (Div): Container
           - `bestsellers-list` (Div): Ranked list of bestsellers
           - `time-period-filter` (Dropdown): Filter by time period
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): View book
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Back to dashboard
         - Context variables: `bestsellers`, `time_period`
         - POST forms for filtering and navigation
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification
         
         ### 1. books.txt
         - File Path: `data/books.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - Fields (in order):
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `title` (str)
           3. `author` (str)
           4. `isbn` (str)
           5. `category` (str)
           6. `price` (float)
           7. `stock` (int)
           8. `description` (str)
         - Description: Complete book records.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
         2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
         3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
         ```
         
         ### 2. categories.txt
         - File Path: `data/categories.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `category_id` (int)
           2. `category_name` (str)
           3. `description` (str)
         - Description: Book categories.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
         2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
         3|Science|Scientific topics and research
         ```
         
         ### 3. cart.txt
         - File Path: `data/cart.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `cart_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `quantity` (int)
           4. `added_date` (date YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Current cart items.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|1|2|2025-01-15
         2|3|1|2025-01-16
         ```
         
         ### 4. orders.txt
         - File Path: `data/orders.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `order_id` (int)
           2. `customer_name` (str)
           3. `order_date` (date YYYY-MM-DD)
           4. `total_amount` (float)
           5. `status` (str)
           6. `shipping_address` (str)
         - Description: Customer orders.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
         2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
         ```
         
         ### 5. order_items.txt
         - File Path: `data/order_items.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `order_item_id` (int)
           2. `order_id` (int)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `quantity` (int)
           5. `price` (float)
         - Description: Items for each order.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|1|1|2|12.99
         2|1|3|1|14.99
         3|2|2|1|16.99
         ```
         
         ### 6. reviews.txt
         - File Path: `data/reviews.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `review_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `customer_name` (str)
           4. `rating` (int 1-5)
           5. `review_text` (str)
           6. `review_date` (date YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Customer reviews.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
         2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
         3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
         ```
         
         ### 7. bestsellers.txt
         - File Path: `data/bestsellers.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `sales_count` (int)
           3. `period` (str) (e.g. This Week, This Month, All Time)
         - Description: Ranked sales data by period.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         2|150|This Month
         1|120|This Month
         3|95|This Month
         ```
         
         ---
         
         This detailed specification enables backend and frontend developers to independently implement BookstoreOnline application with exact routing, template composition, element IDs, and data file specifications.

         Implement HTML design_spec.md 2

         === design_spec.md ===
         # BookstoreOnline Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         ### 1. Dashboard
         - Route Path: `/`
         - Function Name: `dashboard`
         - HTTP Methods: GET
         - Template Rendered: `dashboard.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `featured_books` (List[Dict]): List of featured books with keys `book_id`, `title`, `author`, `price`.
         - POST Behavior: None
         
         ### 2. Book Catalog
         - Route Path: `/catalog`
         - Function Name: `book_catalog`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `catalog.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `books` (List[Dict]): List of books filtered/searched.
           - `categories` (List[Dict]): List of available categories.
           - `selected_category` (str|None): Currently selected category ID or None.
           - `search_query` (str): Current search string.
         - POST Behavior: Handles search and filter submissions, updates displayed books accordingly.
         
         ### 3. Book Details
         - Route Path: `/book/<int:book_id>`
         - Function Name: `book_details`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `details.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` (Dict): Book details.
           - `reviews` (List[Dict]): Related customer reviews for the book.
         - POST Behavior: Allows adding book to cart triggered by button `add-to-cart-button`.
         
         ### 4. Shopping Cart
         - Route Path: `/cart`
         - Function Name: `shopping_cart`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `cart.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `cart_items` (List[Dict]): Cart items, each with `item_id`, `book_id`, `title`, `quantity`, `price`, and `subtotal`.
           - `total_amount` (float): Total cart price.
         - POST Behavior: Handles updates to item quantity via input IDs `update-quantity-{item_id}` and removal of items via buttons `remove-item-button-{item_id}`.
         
         ### 5. Checkout
         - Route Path: `/checkout`
         - Function Name: `checkout`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `checkout.html`
         - Context Variables: None
         - POST Behavior: Processes submitted customer name, shipping address, and payment method via form with `place-order-button`.
         
         ### 6. Order History
         - Route Path: `/orders`
         - Function Name: `order_history`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `history.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `orders` (List[Dict]): List of customer orders.
           - `status_filter` (str): Current status filter (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).
         - POST Behavior: Filtering by order status and viewing order details triggered by button `view-order-button-{order_id}`.
         
         ### 7. Reviews
         - Route Path: `/reviews`
         - Function Name: `reviews`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `reviews.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `reviews` (List[Dict]): Customer reviews.
           - `rating_filter` (str|int): Star rating filter selected.
         - POST Behavior: Filter reviews by rating dropdown, navigate to write review via `write-review-button`.
         
         ### 8. Write Review
         - Route Path: `/write_review`
         - Function Name: `write_review`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `write_review.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `purchased_books` (List[Dict]): Books eligible for reviews.
         - POST Behavior: Review submission handling with fields `select-book`, `rating-select`, `review-text` and `submit-review-button`.
         
         ### 9. Bestsellers
         - Route Path: `/bestsellers`
         - Function Name: `bestsellers`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `bestsellers.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `bestsellers` (List[Dict]): List of bestselling books.
           - `time_period` (str): Selected time period filter.
         - POST Behavior: Handles time period filter and book detail views.
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### dashboard.html
         - File path: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page title: "Bookstore Dashboard"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Bookstore Dashboard</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div): Main container
           - `featured-books` (Div): Displays featured books
           - `browse-catalog-button` (Button): Navigates to `/catalog`
           - `view-cart-button` (Button): Navigates to `/cart`
           - `bestsellers-button` (Button): Navigates to `/bestsellers`
         - Context variables: `featured_books`
         - Navigation via `url_for` calls to respective routes
         - No forms
         
         ### catalog.html
         - File path: `templates/catalog.html`
         - Page title: "Book Catalog"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Book Catalog</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `catalog-page` (Div): Main container
           - `search-input` (Input): Text search input
           - `category-filter` (Dropdown): Category filter
           - `books-grid` (Div): Container for book cards
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): View book details button per book
         - Context variables: `books`, `categories`, `selected_category`, `search_query`
         - Buttons navigation via `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`
         - Search and filter via POST form submission
         
         ### details.html
         - File path: `templates/details.html`
         - Page title: "Book Details"
         - Main heading: `<h1 id="book-title">{{ book.title }}</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `book-details-page` (Div): Container
           - `book-author` (Div): Book author
           - `book-price` (Div): Book price
           - `add-to-cart-button` (Button): Adds book to cart (POST button)
           - `book-reviews` (Div): Displays reviews
         - Context variables: `book`, `reviews`
         - POST form with `add-to-cart-button` to add the book to the cart
         
         ### cart.html
         - File path: `templates/cart.html`
         - Page title: "Shopping Cart"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Shopping Cart</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `cart-page` (Div): Main container
           - `cart-items-table` (Table): Displays cart items
           - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input Number): Quantity input for each cart item
           - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button): Button to remove item from cart
           - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button): Proceeds to checkout
           - `total-amount` (Div): Displays total amount
         - Context variables: `cart_items`, `total_amount`
         - POST forms for quantity update and removal
         
         ### checkout.html
         - File path: `templates/checkout.html`
         - Page title: "Checkout"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Checkout</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `checkout-page` (Div): Container
           - `customer-name` (Input): Customer name input
           - `shipping-address` (Textarea): Shipping address input
           - `payment-method` (Dropdown): Payment method selection
           - `place-order-button` (Button): Submit order
         - Context variables: None
         - POST form submission
         
         ### history.html
         - File path: `templates/history.html`
         - Page title: "Order History"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Order History</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `orders-page` (Div): Container
           - `orders-table` (Table): Table listing order records
           - `view-order-button-{order_id}` (Button): View order details
           - `order-status-filter` (Dropdown): Filter orders by status
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context variables: `orders`, `status_filter`
         - POST form to filter or view order
         
         ### reviews.html
         - File path: `templates/reviews.html`
         - Page title: "Customer Reviews"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Customer Reviews</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `reviews-page` (Div): Container
           - `reviews-list` (Div): Contains all reviews
           - `write-review-button` (Button): Navigate to write review page
           - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown): Filter reviews by rating
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context variables: `reviews`, `rating_filter`
         - POST form submission
         
         ### write_review.html
         - File path: `templates/write_review.html`
         - Page title: "Write a Review"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Write a Review</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `write-review-page` (Div): Container
           - `select-book` (Dropdown): Select book to review
           - `rating-select` (Dropdown): Select rating 1-5
           - `review-text` (Textarea): Input review text
           - `submit-review-button` (Button): Submit review
         - Context variables: `purchased_books`
         - POST form submission
         
         ### bestsellers.html
         - File path: `templates/bestsellers.html`
         - Page title: "Bestsellers"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Bestsellers</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `bestsellers-page` (Div): Container
           - `bestsellers-list` (Div): Ranked list of bestsellers
           - `time-period-filter` (Dropdown): Filter by time period
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): View book
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Back to dashboard
         - Context variables: `bestsellers`, `time_period`
         - POST forms for filtering and navigation
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification
         
         ### 1. books.txt
         - File Path: `data/books.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - Fields (in order):
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `title` (str)
           3. `author` (str)
           4. `isbn` (str)
           5. `category` (str)
           6. `price` (float)
           7. `stock` (int)
           8. `description` (str)
         - Description: Complete book records.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
         2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
         3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
         ```
         
         ### 2. categories.txt
         - File Path: `data/categories.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `category_id` (int)
           2. `category_name` (str)
           3. `description` (str)
         - Description: Book categories.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
         2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
         3|Science|Scientific topics and research
         ```
         
         ### 3. cart.txt
         - File Path: `data/cart.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `cart_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `quantity` (int)
           4. `added_date` (date YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Current cart items.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|1|2|2025-01-15
         2|3|1|2025-01-16
         ```
         
         ### 4. orders.txt
         - File Path: `data/orders.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `order_id` (int)
           2. `customer_name` (str)
           3. `order_date` (date YYYY-MM-DD)
           4. `total_amount` (float)
           5. `status` (str)
           6. `shipping_address` (str)
         - Description: Customer orders.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
         2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
         ```
         
         ### 5. order_items.txt
         - File Path: `data/order_items.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `order_item_id` (int)
           2. `order_id` (int)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `quantity` (int)
           5. `price` (float)
         - Description: Items for each order.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|1|1|2|12.99
         2|1|3|1|14.99
         3|2|2|1|16.99
         ```
         
         ### 6. reviews.txt
         - File Path: `data/reviews.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `review_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `customer_name` (str)
           4. `rating` (int 1-5)
           5. `review_text` (str)
           6. `review_date` (date YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Customer reviews.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
         2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
         3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
         ```
         
         ### 7. bestsellers.txt
         - File Path: `data/bestsellers.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `sales_count` (int)
           3. `period` (str) (e.g. This Week, This Month, All Time)
         - Description: Ranked sales data by period.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         2|150|This Month
         1|120|This Month
         3|95|This Month
         ```
         
         ---
         
         This detailed specification enables backend and frontend developers to independently implement BookstoreOnline application with exact routing, template composition, element IDs, and data file specifications.

         all templates based design_spec.md

      📄 Before (full content):
         Implement all HTML templates based on design_spec.md Section 2
         === design_spec.md ===
         # BookstoreOnline Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         ### 1. Dashboard
         - Route Path: `/`
         - Function Name: `dashboard`
         - HTTP Methods: GET
         - Template Rendered: `dashboard.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `featured_books` (List[Dict]): List of featured books with keys `book_id`, `title`, `author`, `price`.
         - POST Behavior: None
         
         ### 2. Book Catalog
         - Route Path: `/catalog`
         - Function Name: `book_catalog`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `catalog.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `books` (List[Dict]): List of books filtered/searched.
           - `categories` (List[Dict]): List of available categories.
           - `selected_category` (str|None): Currently selected category ID or None.
           - `search_query` (str): Current search string.
         - POST Behavior: Handles search and filter submissions, updates displayed books accordingly.
         
         ### 3. Book Details
         - Route Path: `/book/<int:book_id>`
         - Function Name: `book_details`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `details.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` (Dict): Book details.
           - `reviews` (List[Dict]): Related customer reviews for the book.
         - POST Behavior: Allows adding book to cart triggered by button `add-to-cart-button`.
         
         ### 4. Shopping Cart
         - Route Path: `/cart`
         - Function Name: `shopping_cart`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `cart.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `cart_items` (List[Dict]): Cart items, each with `item_id`, `book_id`, `title`, `quantity`, `price`, and `subtotal`.
           - `total_amount` (float): Total cart price.
         - POST Behavior: Handles updates to item quantity via input IDs `update-quantity-{item_id}` and removal of items via buttons `remove-item-button-{item_id}`.
         
         ### 5. Checkout
         - Route Path: `/checkout`
         - Function Name: `checkout`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `checkout.html`
         - Context Variables: None
         - POST Behavior: Processes submitted customer name, shipping address, and payment method via form with `place-order-button`.
         
         ### 6. Order History
         - Route Path: `/orders`
         - Function Name: `order_history`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `history.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `orders` (List[Dict]): List of customer orders.
           - `status_filter` (str): Current status filter (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).
         - POST Behavior: Filtering by order status and viewing order details triggered by button `view-order-button-{order_id}`.
         
         ### 7. Reviews
         - Route Path: `/reviews`
         - Function Name: `reviews`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `reviews.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `reviews` (List[Dict]): Customer reviews.
           - `rating_filter` (str|int): Star rating filter selected.
         - POST Behavior: Filter reviews by rating dropdown, navigate to write review via `write-review-button`.
         
         ### 8. Write Review
         - Route Path: `/write_review`
         - Function Name: `write_review`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `write_review.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `purchased_books` (List[Dict]): Books eligible for reviews.
         - POST Behavior: Review submission handling with fields `select-book`, `rating-select`, `review-text` and `submit-review-button`.
         
         ### 9. Bestsellers
         - Route Path: `/bestsellers`
         - Function Name: `bestsellers`
         - HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Template Rendered: `bestsellers.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `bestsellers` (List[Dict]): List of bestselling books.
           - `time_period` (str): Selected time period filter.
         - POST Behavior: Handles time period filter and book detail views.
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### dashboard.html
         - File path: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page title: "Bookstore Dashboard"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Bookstore Dashboard</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div): Main container
           - `featured-books` (Div): Displays featured books
           - `browse-catalog-button` (Button): Navigates to `/catalog`
           - `view-cart-button` (Button): Navigates to `/cart`
           - `bestsellers-button` (Button): Navigates to `/bestsellers`
         - Context variables: `featured_books`
         - Navigation via `url_for` calls to respective routes
         - No forms
         
         ### catalog.html
         - File path: `templates/catalog.html`
         - Page title: "Book Catalog"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Book Catalog</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `catalog-page` (Div): Main container
           - `search-input` (Input): Text search input
           - `category-filter` (Dropdown): Category filter
           - `books-grid` (Div): Container for book cards
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): View book details button per book
         - Context variables: `books`, `categories`, `selected_category`, `search_query`
         - Buttons navigation via `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`
         - Search and filter via POST form submission
         
         ### details.html
         - File path: `templates/details.html`
         - Page title: "Book Details"
         - Main heading: `<h1 id="book-title">{{ book.title }}</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `book-details-page` (Div): Container
           - `book-author` (Div): Book author
           - `book-price` (Div): Book price
           - `add-to-cart-button` (Button): Adds book to cart (POST button)
           - `book-reviews` (Div): Displays reviews
         - Context variables: `book`, `reviews`
         - POST form with `add-to-cart-button` to add the book to the cart
         
         ### cart.html
         - File path: `templates/cart.html`
         - Page title: "Shopping Cart"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Shopping Cart</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `cart-page` (Div): Main container
           - `cart-items-table` (Table): Displays cart items
           - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input Number): Quantity input for each cart item
           - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button): Button to remove item from cart
           - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button): Proceeds to checkout
           - `total-amount` (Div): Displays total amount
         - Context variables: `cart_items`, `total_amount`
         - POST forms for quantity update and removal
         
         ### checkout.html
         - File path: `templates/checkout.html`
         - Page title: "Checkout"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Checkout</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `checkout-page` (Div): Container
           - `customer-name` (Input): Customer name input
           - `shipping-address` (Textarea): Shipping address input
           - `payment-method` (Dropdown): Payment method selection
           - `place-order-button` (Button): Submit order
         - Context variables: None
         - POST form submission
         
         ### history.html
         - File path: `templates/history.html`
         - Page title: "Order History"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Order History</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `orders-page` (Div): Container
           - `orders-table` (Table): Table listing order records
           - `view-order-button-{order_id}` (Button): View order details
           - `order-status-filter` (Dropdown): Filter orders by status
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context variables: `orders`, `status_filter`
         - POST form to filter or view order
         
         ### reviews.html
         - File path: `templates/reviews.html`
         - Page title: "Customer Reviews"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Customer Reviews</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `reviews-page` (Div): Container
           - `reviews-list` (Div): Contains all reviews
           - `write-review-button` (Button): Navigate to write review page
           - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown): Filter reviews by rating
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context variables: `reviews`, `rating_filter`
         - POST form submission
         
         ### write_review.html
         - File path: `templates/write_review.html`
         - Page title: "Write a Review"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Write a Review</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `write-review-page` (Div): Container
           - `select-book` (Dropdown): Select book to review
           - `rating-select` (Dropdown): Select rating 1-5
           - `review-text` (Textarea): Input review text
           - `submit-review-button` (Button): Submit review
         - Context variables: `purchased_books`
         - POST form submission
         
         ### bestsellers.html
         - File path: `templates/bestsellers.html`
         - Page title: "Bestsellers"
         - Main heading: `<h1>Bestsellers</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `bestsellers-page` (Div): Container
           - `bestsellers-list` (Div): Ranked list of bestsellers
           - `time-period-filter` (Dropdown): Filter by time period
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button): View book
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Back to dashboard
         - Context variables: `bestsellers`, `time_period`
         - POST forms for filtering and navigation
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification
         
         ### 1. books.txt
         - File Path: `data/books.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - Fields (in order):
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `title` (str)
           3. `author` (str)
           4. `isbn` (str)
           5. `category` (str)
           6. `price` (float)
           7. `stock` (int)
           8. `description` (str)
         - Description: Complete book records.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
         2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
         3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
         ```
         
         ### 2. categories.txt
         - File Path: `data/categories.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `category_id` (int)
           2. `category_name` (str)
           3. `description` (str)
         - Description: Book categories.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
         2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
         3|Science|Scientific topics and research
         ```
         
         ### 3. cart.txt
         - File Path: `data/cart.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `cart_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `quantity` (int)
           4. `added_date` (date YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Current cart items.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|1|2|2025-01-15
         2|3|1|2025-01-16
         ```
         
         ### 4. orders.txt
         - File Path: `data/orders.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `order_id` (int)
           2. `customer_name` (str)
           3. `order_date` (date YYYY-MM-DD)
           4. `total_amount` (float)
           5. `status` (str)
           6. `shipping_address` (str)
         - Description: Customer orders.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
         2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
         ```
         
         ### 5. order_items.txt
         - File Path: `data/order_items.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `order_item_id` (int)
           2. `order_id` (int)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `quantity` (int)
           5. `price` (float)
         - Description: Items for each order.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|1|1|2|12.99
         2|1|3|1|14.99
         3|2|2|1|16.99
         ```
         
         ### 6. reviews.txt
         - File Path: `data/reviews.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `review_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `customer_name` (str)
           4. `rating` (int 1-5)
           5. `review_text` (str)
           6. `review_date` (date YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Customer reviews.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
         2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
         3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
         ```
         
         ### 7. bestsellers.txt
         - File Path: `data/bestsellers.txt`
         - Format: Pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `sales_count` (int)
           3. `period` (str) (e.g. This Week, This Month, All Time)
         - Description: Ranked sales data by period.
         - Example Rows:
         ```
         2|150|This Month
         1|120|This Month
         3|95|This Month
         ```
         
         ---
         
         This detailed specification enables backend and frontend developers to independently implement BookstoreOnline application with exact routing, template composition, element IDs, and data file specifications.

         # BookstoreOnline Design Specification
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes
         
         ### 1. Root Dashboard
         - **Path:** `/`
         - **Function Name:** `dashboard`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`
         - **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
         - **Variables:** None
         - **Description:** Main hub, displays buttons to navigate to catalog page, and view cart.
         
         ### 2. Book Catalog
         - **Path:** `/catalog`
         - **Function Name:** `catalog`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `books`: List of books filtered/searched.
           - `categories`: List of categories for filter dropdown.
           - `selected_category`: Currently filtered category id or None.
           - `search_query`: Current search string.
         - **Description:** Displays all books with filter and search features.
           - POST used for filtering by category or searching.
           - Each book item includes button with id `view-book-button-{book_id}` to view details.
           - Form includes add to cart button for each book (via details page). 
         
         ### 3. Book Details
         - **Path:** `/details/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `details`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `details.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `book`: Book detail dict.
         - **Description:** Shows detailed book info including title, author, price, description.
           - Button with id `add-to-cart-button` to add book to cart (POST).
         
         ### 4. Cart
         - **Path:** `/cart`
         - **Function Name:** `cart`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `cart.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `cart_items`: List of items with quantity, price, subtotal.
           - `total_amount`: Total price.
         - **Description:** Display cart contents.
           - Forms/buttons to update quantity per item.
           - Button with id `proceed-checkout-button` to proceed checkout.
         
         ### 5. Checkout
         - **Path:** `/checkout`
         - **Function Name:** `checkout`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`
         - **Variables:** None
         - **Description:** Form to input customer name, shipping address, and payment method (dropdown). 
           - Confirm button submits order.
         
         ### 6. Order History
         - **Path:** `/history`
         - **Function Name:** `history`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`
         - **Template Rendered:** `history.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `orders`: List of user orders with order date, total, status.
         - **Description:** Displays previous orders with detail buttons.
           - Dropdown filter by order status.
         
         ### 7. Reviews List
         - **Path:** `/reviews`
         - **Function Name:** `reviews`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`
         - **Template Rendered:** `reviews.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `reviews`: List of reviews.
           - `rating_filter`: Filter rating selected.
         - **Description:** Displays customer reviews with filters by star rating.
           - Back to dashboard button.
         
         ### 8. Write Review
         - **Path:** `/write_review`
         - **Function Name:** `write_review`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `books`: List of purchased books for dropdown.
         - **Description:** Form to submit a review with dropdown `select-book`, rating selector (1-5), and text.
         
         ### 9. Bestsellers
         - **Path:** `/bestsellers`
         - **Function Name:** `bestsellers`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `bestsellers.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `bestsellers`: List of books ranked by sales.
           - `time_period`: Selected filter period.
         - **Description:** Displays ranked bestselling books, filterable by time period.
           - Buttons to view book details.
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Templates
         
         ### 1. dashboard.html (templates/dashboard.html)
         - **Purpose:** Home page with navigation buttons.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#dashboard-page`: Main container for dashboard.
           - `button#browse-catalog-button`: Button to navigate to `/catalog`.
           - `button#view-cart-button`: Button to navigate to `/cart`.
         
         ### 2. catalog.html (templates/catalog.html)
         - **Purpose:** Display and filter/search book catalog.
         - **Elements:**
           - `input#search-box` (text input): Search books by title or author.
           - `select#category-filter`: Dropdown to select category filter.
           - For each book:
             - `div.book-item`: Container showing cover (if any), title, author, price.
             - `button#view-book-button-{book_id}`: Button to view detailed page.
         
         ### 3. details.html (templates/details.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show book details.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#book-details-page`: Container.
           - `h1#book-title`: Book title.
           - `div#book-author`: Book author.
           - `div#book-description`: Description text.
           - `button#add-to-cart-button`: Add book to cart.
         
         ### 4. cart.html (templates/cart.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show cart items and facilitate quantity update and checkout.
         - **Elements:**
           - Table/list with cart items: title, quantity (with input), price, subtotal.
           - Update quantity buttons/forms per item.
           - `button#proceed-checkout-button`: Button to proceed to checkout.
           - Display total amount.
         
         ### 5. checkout.html (templates/checkout.html)
         - **Purpose:** Form to complete purchase.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#checkout-page`: Container.
           - `input#customer-name`: Text field for customer.
           - `textarea#shipping-address`: Shipping address input.
           - `select#payment-method`: Dropdown (e.g., "Credit Card", "Bank Transfer").
           - Confirm button submits form.
         
         ### 6. history.html (templates/history.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show past orders.
         - **Elements:**
           - List/table of orders: date, total amount, status.
           - Dropdown to filter by order status.
           - Detail buttons for each order.
           - Button `back-to-dashboard` to return.
         
         ### 7. reviews.html (templates/reviews.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show customer reviews.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#reviews-page`: Container.
           - Reviews list with rating stars, review text, date.
           - Dropdown to filter by stars.
           - Button `back-to-dashboard`.
         
         ### 8. write_review.html (templates/write_review.html)
         - **Purpose:** Form for submitting book review.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#write-review-page`: Container.
           - `select#select-book`: Dropdown of purchased books.
           - `select#rating`: Dropdown from 1 to 5.
           - `textarea#review-text`: Text input area.
           - Submit button to post review.
         
         ### 9. bestsellers.html (templates/bestsellers.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show bestselling books ranked.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#bestsellers-page`: Container.
           - List of rank, title, sales count.
           - `select#time-period-filter`: Dropdown for Month, Year, All Time.
           - Each book has a details button.
           - Button `back-to-dashboard`.
         
         All navigation buttons use `url_for()` for links and forms where applicable.
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Specifications
         
         ### 1. books.txt
         - **Path:** `data/books.txt`
         - **Fields:** 
           - `book_id` (int), `title` (str), `author` (str), `isbn` (str), `category` (int), `price` (float), `stock` (int), `description` (str)
         - **Description:** Contains all book details.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|1|10.99|15|Classic social novel.
           ```
         
         ### 2. categories.txt
         - **Path:** `data/categories.txt`
         - **Fields:** 
           - `category_id` (int), `category_name` (str), `description` (str)
         - **Description:** Categories for books.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|Fiction|Fictional novels
           2|Non-Fiction|Educational and factual
           3|Science|Scientific and research texts
           ```
         
         ### 3. orders.txt
         - **Path:** `data/orders.txt`
         - **Fields:**
           - `order_id` (int), `customer_name` (str), `order_date` (date yyyy-mm-dd), `total_amount` (float), `status` (str), `shipping_address` (str)
         - **Description:** Customer order records.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|John Doe|2025-01-16|59.97|Pending|123 Main St, Los Angeles
           ```
         
         ### 4. order_items.txt
         - **Path:** `data/order_items.txt`
         - **Fields:**
           - `order_item_id` (int), `order_id` (int), `book_id` (int), `quantity` (int), `price_each` (float)
         - **Description:** Items included in each order.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|1|3|2|19.99
           ```
         
         ### 5. reviews.txt
         - **Path:** `data/reviews.txt`
         - **Fields:**
           - `review_id` (int), `book_id` (int), `customer_name` (str), `rating` (int 1-5), `review_text` (str), `review_date` (date yyyy-mm-dd)
         - **Description:** Customer reviews.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           5|2|Alice|5|Amazing book! A classic.|2025-01-12
           ```
         
         ### 6. bestsellers.txt
         - **Path:** `data/bestsellers.txt`
         - **Fields:**
           - `rank` (int), `book_id` (int), `sales` (int), `period` (str)
         - **Description:** Ranked bestsellers by period.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|2|150|Month
           3|5|95|Month
           ```
         
         ---
         
         This specification covers all Flask routes with route details, frontend HTML template element IDs and roles, and the data file schemas with example data lines.

         # BookstoreOnline Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes
         
         ### 1. Dashboard
         - **URL Path:** `/`
         - **Function Name:** `dashboard`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET
         - **Rendered Template:** `dashboard.html`
         - **Context Variables:** None
         - **Description:** The main dashboard page presenting navigation buttons to catalog, cart, and bestsellers.
         
         ### 2. Catalog
         - **URL Path:** `/catalog`
         - **Function Name:** `catalog`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `catalog.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `books`: list of book dicts filtered by category or search query
           - `categories`: list of all categories
           - `selected_category`: currently selected category id or None
           - `search_query`: current search input string
         - **Description:** Shows all books with search and category filtering functionality. Each book card has button to navigate to details page.
         
         ### 3. Book Details
         - **URL Path:** `/details/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `details`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `details.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `book`: dict of book details
         - **Description:** Displays detailed information about a selected book with an "Add to Cart" button.
         
         ### 4. Shopping Cart
         - **URL Path:** `/cart`
         - **Function Name:** `cart`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `cart.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `cart_items`: list of dictionaries with cart item details including quantity
           - `total_amount`: computed total price in the cart
         - **Description:** Shows all items in cart with quantity update inputs and a checkout button.
         
         ### 5. Checkout
         - **URL Path:** `/checkout`
         - **Function Name:** `checkout`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `checkout.html`
         - **Context Variables:** None
         - **Description:** Form for customers to input name, shipping address and select payment method. Allows order submission.
         
         ### 6. Order History
         - **URL Path:** `/history`
         - **Function Name:** `order_history`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET
         - **Rendered Template:** `history.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `orders`: list of orders with date, total amount, status
         - **Description:** Displays customer past orders with a status filter dropdown and buttons to view order details.
         
         ### 7. Reviews
         - **URL Path:** `/reviews`
         - **Function Name:** `reviews`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET
         - **Rendered Template:** `reviews.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reviews`: list of review dicts filtered by rating
           - `rating_filter`: selected rating filter
         - **Description:** Shows all customer reviews with the ability to filter by star rating. Includes write review button.
         
         ### 8. Write Review
         - **URL Path:** `/write_review`
         - **Function Name:** `write_review`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `write_review.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `purchased_books`: list of books eligible for review
         - **Description:** Allows user to select a purchased book, add star rating and textual review.
         
         ### 9. Bestsellers
         - **URL Path:** `/bestsellers`
         - **Function Name:** `bestsellers`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `bestsellers.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `bestseller_books`: list of bestseller book dicts
           - `time_period`: selected filter period (e.g., Month, Year, All)
         - **Description:** Displays bestselling books ranked by sales with a time period filter and view details buttons.
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Templates Details
         
         ### Template: dashboard.html (templates/dashboard.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Dashboard"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#dashboard-page` (Container div)
           - `button#catalog-button` - Navigate to catalog page
           - `button#view-cart-button` - Navigate to cart page
           - `button#bestsellers-button` - Navigate to bestsellers page
         
         ### Template: catalog.html (templates/catalog.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Book Catalog"
         - **Elements:**
           - `input#search-input` (text) - Search input box for book title/author
           - `select#category-filter` - Dropdown to filter books by category
           - `div#books-grid` - Grid container listing books
           - Each book entry includes:
             - Cover image (optional)
             - Title and author text
             - Price display
             - `button#view-book-button-{book_id}` to open details page
         
         ### Template: details.html (templates/details.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Book Details"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#book-details-page` (Container div)
           - `h1#book-title` - Book title
           - `div#book-author` - Author name
           - `div#book-description` - Detailed description
           - `button#add-to-cart-button` - Add book to shopping cart
         
         ### Template: cart.html (templates/cart.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Shopping Cart"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#cart-page` (Container div)
           - `table#cart-items-table` with rows per item including:
             - Book name
             - Quantity input number with `id=update-quantity-{item_id}`
             - Price per unit
             - Subtotal
           - `div#total-amount` showing total cart price
           - `button#checkout-button` - Proceed to checkout
         
         ### Template: checkout.html (templates/checkout.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Checkout"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#checkout-page` (Container div)
           - `input#customer-name` - Text input for customer name
           - `textarea#shipping-address` - Shipping address field
           - `select#payment-method` - Dropdown with options (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer)
           - `button#place-order-button` - Confirm and place order
         
         ### Template: history.html (templates/history.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Order History"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#history-page` (Container div)
           - `select#status-filter` - Dropdown to filter orders by status (All, Delivered, Pending, etc.)
           - List or table showing order date, total amount, and status
           - `button#view-order-button-{order_id}` - Button to view order details
           - `button#back-to-dashboard` - Return to dashboard
         
         ### Template: reviews.html (templates/reviews.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Reviews"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#reviews-page` (Container div)
           - `select#rating-filter` - Dropdown to filter by stars (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.)
           - List `ul#reviews-list` showing reviews with title, rating stars, text
           - `button#write-review-button` - Navigate to write a review page
           - `button#back-to-dashboard` - Return to dashboard
         
         ### Template: write_review.html (templates/write_review.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Write a Review"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#write-review-page` (Container div)
           - `select#select-book` - Dropdown of purchased books
           - `select#select-rating` - Dropdown with rating 1 to 5
           - `textarea#review-text` - Text input for review comments
           - `button#submit-review-button` - Submit review
         
         ### Template: bestsellers.html (templates/bestsellers.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Bestsellers"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#bestsellers-page` (Container div)
           - `select#time-period-filter` - Dropdown to filter by period (This Month, This Year, All Time)
           - List with ranking number, book title, author, sales count
           - `button#view-bestseller-button-{book_id}` - Button to view book details
           - `button#back-to-dashboard` - Return to dashboard
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data Files and Schemas
         
         ### 1. books.txt
         - **Location:** `data/books.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated fields
         - **Fields:**
           1. `book_id` (int): Unique book identifier
           2. `title` (str): Book title
           3. `author` (str): Author's name
           4. `isbn` (str): ISBN code
           5. `category` (str): Category name
           6. `price` (float): Book price
           7. `stock` (int): Available stock quantity
           8. `description` (str): Book description
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian fiction
           ```
         
         ### 2. categories.txt
         - **Location:** `data/categories.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `category_id` (int)
           2. `category_name` (str)
           3. `description` (str)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           1|Fiction|Fictional novels
           ```
         
         ### 3. cart.txt
         - **Location:** `data/cart.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `cart_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `quantity` (int)
           4. `added_date` (date `YYYY-MM-DD`)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           2|3|1|2025-01-16
           ```
         
         ### 4. orders.txt
         - **Location:** `data/orders.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `order_id` (int)
           2. `customer_name` (str)
           3. `order_date` (date `YYYY-MM-DD`)
           4. `total_amount` (float)
           5. `status` (str)
           6. `shipping_address` (str)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 St, NY 10001
           ```
         
         ### 5. order_items.txt
         - **Location:** `data/order_items.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `order_item_id` (int)
           2. `order_id` (int)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `quantity` (int)
           5. `price` (float)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           1|1|2|1|19.99
           ```
         
         ### 6. reviews.txt
         - **Location:** `data/reviews.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `review_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `customer_name` (str)
           4. `rating` (int 1-5)
           5. `review_text` (str)
           6. `review_date` (date `YYYY-MM-DD`)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing, very insightful.|2025-01-12
           ```
         
         ### 7. bestsellers.txt
         - **Location:** `data/bestsellers.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `rank` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `sales` (int)
           4. `period` (str; e.g., Month, Year, All Time)
         - **Example Rows:**
           ```
           1|2|150|Month
           3|5|95|Month
           ```
         
         ---
         
         This document defines the core Flask application routes, HTML template structures with element ids for interaction, and the exact data schemas required for the BookstoreOnline application.
