         # BookstoreOnline Design Specification
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes
         
         ### 1. Root Dashboard
         - **Path:** `/`
         - **Function Name:** `dashboard`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`
         - **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
         - **Variables:** None
         - **Description:** Main hub, displays buttons to navigate to catalog page, and view cart.
         
         ### 2. Book Catalog
         - **Path:** `/catalog`
         - **Function Name:** `catalog`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `books`: List of books filtered/searched.
           - `categories`: List of categories for filter dropdown.
           - `selected_category`: Currently filtered category id or None.
           - `search_query`: Current search string.
         - **Description:** Displays all books with filter and search features.
           - POST used for filtering by category or searching.
           - Each book item includes button with id `view-book-button-{book_id}` to view details.
           - Form includes add to cart button for each book (via details page). 
         
         ### 3. Book Details
         - **Path:** `/details/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `details`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `details.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `book`: Book detail dict.
         - **Description:** Shows detailed book info including title, author, price, description.
           - Button with id `add-to-cart-button` to add book to cart (POST).
         
         ### 4. Cart
         - **Path:** `/cart`
         - **Function Name:** `cart`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `cart.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `cart_items`: List of items with quantity, price, subtotal.
           - `total_amount`: Total price.
         - **Description:** Display cart contents.
           - Forms/buttons to update quantity per item.
           - Button with id `proceed-checkout-button` to proceed checkout.
         
         ### 5. Checkout
         - **Path:** `/checkout`
         - **Function Name:** `checkout`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`
         - **Variables:** None
         - **Description:** Form to input customer name, shipping address, and payment method (dropdown). 
           - Confirm button submits order.
         
         ### 6. Order History
         - **Path:** `/history`
         - **Function Name:** `history`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`
         - **Template Rendered:** `history.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `orders`: List of user orders with order date, total, status.
         - **Description:** Displays previous orders with detail buttons.
           - Dropdown filter by order status.
         
         ### 7. Reviews List
         - **Path:** `/reviews`
         - **Function Name:** `reviews`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`
         - **Template Rendered:** `reviews.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `reviews`: List of reviews.
           - `rating_filter`: Filter rating selected.
         - **Description:** Displays customer reviews with filters by star rating.
           - Back to dashboard button.
         
         ### 8. Write Review
         - **Path:** `/write_review`
         - **Function Name:** `write_review`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `books`: List of purchased books for dropdown.
         - **Description:** Form to submit a review with dropdown `select-book`, rating selector (1-5), and text.
         
         ### 9. Bestsellers
         - **Path:** `/bestsellers`
         - **Function Name:** `bestsellers`
         - **HTTP Methods:** `GET`, `POST`
         - **Template Rendered:** `bestsellers.html`
         - **Variables:**
           - `bestsellers`: List of books ranked by sales.
           - `time_period`: Selected filter period.
         - **Description:** Displays ranked bestselling books, filterable by time period.
           - Buttons to view book details.
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Templates
         
         ### 1. dashboard.html (templates/dashboard.html)
         - **Purpose:** Home page with navigation buttons.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#dashboard-page`: Main container for dashboard.
           - `button#browse-catalog-button`: Button to navigate to `/catalog`.
           - `button#view-cart-button`: Button to navigate to `/cart`.
         
         ### 2. catalog.html (templates/catalog.html)
         - **Purpose:** Display and filter/search book catalog.
         - **Elements:**
           - `input#search-box` (text input): Search books by title or author.
           - `select#category-filter`: Dropdown to select category filter.
           - For each book:
             - `div.book-item`: Container showing cover (if any), title, author, price.
             - `button#view-book-button-{book_id}`: Button to view detailed page.
         
         ### 3. details.html (templates/details.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show book details.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#book-details-page`: Container.
           - `h1#book-title`: Book title.
           - `div#book-author`: Book author.
           - `div#book-description`: Description text.
           - `button#add-to-cart-button`: Add book to cart.
         
         ### 4. cart.html (templates/cart.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show cart items and facilitate quantity update and checkout.
         - **Elements:**
           - Table/list with cart items: title, quantity (with input), price, subtotal.
           - Update quantity buttons/forms per item.
           - `button#proceed-checkout-button`: Button to proceed to checkout.
           - Display total amount.
         
         ### 5. checkout.html (templates/checkout.html)
         - **Purpose:** Form to complete purchase.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#checkout-page`: Container.
           - `input#customer-name`: Text field for customer.
           - `textarea#shipping-address`: Shipping address input.
           - `select#payment-method`: Dropdown (e.g., "Credit Card", "Bank Transfer").
           - Confirm button submits form.
         
         ### 6. history.html (templates/history.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show past orders.
         - **Elements:**
           - List/table of orders: date, total amount, status.
           - Dropdown to filter by order status.
           - Detail buttons for each order.
           - Button `back-to-dashboard` to return.
         
         ### 7. reviews.html (templates/reviews.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show customer reviews.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#reviews-page`: Container.
           - Reviews list with rating stars, review text, date.
           - Dropdown to filter by stars.
           - Button `back-to-dashboard`.
         
         ### 8. write_review.html (templates/write_review.html)
         - **Purpose:** Form for submitting book review.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#write-review-page`: Container.
           - `select#select-book`: Dropdown of purchased books.
           - `select#rating`: Dropdown from 1 to 5.
           - `textarea#review-text`: Text input area.
           - Submit button to post review.
         
         ### 9. bestsellers.html (templates/bestsellers.html)
         - **Purpose:** Show bestselling books ranked.
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#bestsellers-page`: Container.
           - List of rank, title, sales count.
           - `select#time-period-filter`: Dropdown for Month, Year, All Time.
           - Each book has a details button.
           - Button `back-to-dashboard`.
         
         All navigation buttons use `url_for()` for links and forms where applicable.
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Specifications
         
         ### 1. books.txt
         - **Path:** `data/books.txt`
         - **Fields:** 
           - `book_id` (int), `title` (str), `author` (str), `isbn` (str), `category` (int), `price` (float), `stock` (int), `description` (str)
         - **Description:** Contains all book details.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|1|10.99|15|Classic social novel.
           ```
         
         ### 2. categories.txt
         - **Path:** `data/categories.txt`
         - **Fields:** 
           - `category_id` (int), `category_name` (str), `description` (str)
         - **Description:** Categories for books.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|Fiction|Fictional novels
           2|Non-Fiction|Educational and factual
           3|Science|Scientific and research texts
           ```
         
         ### 3. orders.txt
         - **Path:** `data/orders.txt`
         - **Fields:**
           - `order_id` (int), `customer_name` (str), `order_date` (date yyyy-mm-dd), `total_amount` (float), `status` (str), `shipping_address` (str)
         - **Description:** Customer order records.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|John Doe|2025-01-16|59.97|Pending|123 Main St, Los Angeles
           ```
         
         ### 4. order_items.txt
         - **Path:** `data/order_items.txt`
         - **Fields:**
           - `order_item_id` (int), `order_id` (int), `book_id` (int), `quantity` (int), `price_each` (float)
         - **Description:** Items included in each order.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|1|3|2|19.99
           ```
         
         ### 5. reviews.txt
         - **Path:** `data/reviews.txt`
         - **Fields:**
           - `review_id` (int), `book_id` (int), `customer_name` (str), `rating` (int 1-5), `review_text` (str), `review_date` (date yyyy-mm-dd)
         - **Description:** Customer reviews.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           5|2|Alice|5|Amazing book! A classic.|2025-01-12
           ```
         
         ### 6. bestsellers.txt
         - **Path:** `data/bestsellers.txt`
         - **Fields:**
           - `rank` (int), `book_id` (int), `sales` (int), `period` (str)
         - **Description:** Ranked bestsellers by period.
         - **Example:**
           ```
           1|2|150|Month
           3|5|95|Month
           ```
         
         ---
         
         This specification covers all Flask routes with route details, frontend HTML template element IDs and roles, and the data file schemas with example data lines.

      📄 Before (full content):
         # BookstoreOnline Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes
         
         ### 1. Dashboard
         - **URL Path:** `/`
         - **Function Name:** `dashboard`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET
         - **Rendered Template:** `dashboard.html`
         - **Context Variables:** None
         - **Description:** The main dashboard page presenting navigation buttons to catalog, cart, and bestsellers.
         
         ### 2. Catalog
         - **URL Path:** `/catalog`
         - **Function Name:** `catalog`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `catalog.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `books`: list of book dicts filtered by category or search query
           - `categories`: list of all categories
           - `selected_category`: currently selected category id or None
           - `search_query`: current search input string
         - **Description:** Shows all books with search and category filtering functionality. Each book card has button to navigate to details page.
         
         ### 3. Book Details
         - **URL Path:** `/details/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `details`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `details.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `book`: dict of book details
         - **Description:** Displays detailed information about a selected book with an "Add to Cart" button.
         
         ### 4. Shopping Cart
         - **URL Path:** `/cart`
         - **Function Name:** `cart`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `cart.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `cart_items`: list of dictionaries with cart item details including quantity
           - `total_amount`: computed total price in the cart
         - **Description:** Shows all items in cart with quantity update inputs and a checkout button.
         
         ### 5. Checkout
         - **URL Path:** `/checkout`
         - **Function Name:** `checkout`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `checkout.html`
         - **Context Variables:** None
         - **Description:** Form for customers to input name, shipping address and select payment method. Allows order submission.
         
         ### 6. Order History
         - **URL Path:** `/history`
         - **Function Name:** `order_history`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET
         - **Rendered Template:** `history.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `orders`: list of orders with date, total amount, status
         - **Description:** Displays customer past orders with a status filter dropdown and buttons to view order details.
         
         ### 7. Reviews
         - **URL Path:** `/reviews`
         - **Function Name:** `reviews`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET
         - **Rendered Template:** `reviews.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reviews`: list of review dicts filtered by rating
           - `rating_filter`: selected rating filter
         - **Description:** Shows all customer reviews with the ability to filter by star rating. Includes write review button.
         
         ### 8. Write Review
         - **URL Path:** `/write_review`
         - **Function Name:** `write_review`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `write_review.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `purchased_books`: list of books eligible for review
         - **Description:** Allows user to select a purchased book, add star rating and textual review.
         
         ### 9. Bestsellers
         - **URL Path:** `/bestsellers`
         - **Function Name:** `bestsellers`
         - **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
         - **Rendered Template:** `bestsellers.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `bestseller_books`: list of bestseller book dicts
           - `time_period`: selected filter period (e.g., Month, Year, All)
         - **Description:** Displays bestselling books ranked by sales with a time period filter and view details buttons.
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Templates Details
         
         ### Template: dashboard.html (templates/dashboard.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Dashboard"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#dashboard-page` (Container div)
           - `button#catalog-button` - Navigate to catalog page
           - `button#view-cart-button` - Navigate to cart page
           - `button#bestsellers-button` - Navigate to bestsellers page
         
         ### Template: catalog.html (templates/catalog.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Book Catalog"
         - **Elements:**
           - `input#search-input` (text) - Search input box for book title/author
           - `select#category-filter` - Dropdown to filter books by category
           - `div#books-grid` - Grid container listing books
           - Each book entry includes:
             - Cover image (optional)
             - Title and author text
             - Price display
             - `button#view-book-button-{book_id}` to open details page
         
         ### Template: details.html (templates/details.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Book Details"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#book-details-page` (Container div)
           - `h1#book-title` - Book title
           - `div#book-author` - Author name
           - `div#book-description` - Detailed description
           - `button#add-to-cart-button` - Add book to shopping cart
         
         ### Template: cart.html (templates/cart.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Shopping Cart"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#cart-page` (Container div)
           - `table#cart-items-table` with rows per item including:
             - Book name
             - Quantity input number with `id=update-quantity-{item_id}`
             - Price per unit
             - Subtotal
           - `div#total-amount` showing total cart price
           - `button#checkout-button` - Proceed to checkout
         
         ### Template: checkout.html (templates/checkout.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Checkout"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#checkout-page` (Container div)
           - `input#customer-name` - Text input for customer name
           - `textarea#shipping-address` - Shipping address field
           - `select#payment-method` - Dropdown with options (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer)
           - `button#place-order-button` - Confirm and place order
         
         ### Template: history.html (templates/history.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Order History"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#history-page` (Container div)
           - `select#status-filter` - Dropdown to filter orders by status (All, Delivered, Pending, etc.)
           - List or table showing order date, total amount, and status
           - `button#view-order-button-{order_id}` - Button to view order details
           - `button#back-to-dashboard` - Return to dashboard
         
         ### Template: reviews.html (templates/reviews.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Reviews"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#reviews-page` (Container div)
           - `select#rating-filter` - Dropdown to filter by stars (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.)
           - List `ul#reviews-list` showing reviews with title, rating stars, text
           - `button#write-review-button` - Navigate to write a review page
           - `button#back-to-dashboard` - Return to dashboard
         
         ### Template: write_review.html (templates/write_review.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Write a Review"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#write-review-page` (Container div)
           - `select#select-book` - Dropdown of purchased books
           - `select#select-rating` - Dropdown with rating 1 to 5
           - `textarea#review-text` - Text input for review comments
           - `button#submit-review-button` - Submit review
         
         ### Template: bestsellers.html (templates/bestsellers.html)
         - **Page Title:** "Bestsellers"
         - **Elements:**
           - `div#bestsellers-page` (Container div)
           - `select#time-period-filter` - Dropdown to filter by period (This Month, This Year, All Time)
           - List with ranking number, book title, author, sales count
           - `button#view-bestseller-button-{book_id}` - Button to view book details
           - `button#back-to-dashboard` - Return to dashboard
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data Files and Schemas
         
         ### 1. books.txt
         - **Location:** `data/books.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated fields
         - **Fields:**
           1. `book_id` (int): Unique book identifier
           2. `title` (str): Book title
           3. `author` (str): Author's name
           4. `isbn` (str): ISBN code
           5. `category` (str): Category name
           6. `price` (float): Book price
           7. `stock` (int): Available stock quantity
           8. `description` (str): Book description
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian fiction
           ```
         
         ### 2. categories.txt
         - **Location:** `data/categories.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `category_id` (int)
           2. `category_name` (str)
           3. `description` (str)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           1|Fiction|Fictional novels
           ```
         
         ### 3. cart.txt
         - **Location:** `data/cart.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `cart_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `quantity` (int)
           4. `added_date` (date `YYYY-MM-DD`)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           2|3|1|2025-01-16
           ```
         
         ### 4. orders.txt
         - **Location:** `data/orders.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `order_id` (int)
           2. `customer_name` (str)
           3. `order_date` (date `YYYY-MM-DD`)
           4. `total_amount` (float)
           5. `status` (str)
           6. `shipping_address` (str)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 St, NY 10001
           ```
         
         ### 5. order_items.txt
         - **Location:** `data/order_items.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `order_item_id` (int)
           2. `order_id` (int)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `quantity` (int)
           5. `price` (float)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           1|1|2|1|19.99
           ```
         
         ### 6. reviews.txt
         - **Location:** `data/reviews.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `review_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `customer_name` (str)
           4. `rating` (int 1-5)
           5. `review_text` (str)
           6. `review_date` (date `YYYY-MM-DD`)
         - **Example Row:**
           ```
           1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing, very insightful.|2025-01-12
           ```
         
         ### 7. bestsellers.txt
         - **Location:** `data/bestsellers.txt`
         - **Format:** pipe-separated
         - **Fields:**
           1. `rank` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `sales` (int)
           4. `period` (str; e.g., Month, Year, All Time)
         - **Example Rows:**
           ```
           1|2|150|Month
           3|5|95|Month
           ```
         
         ---
         
         This document defines the core Flask application routes, HTML template structures with element ids for interaction, and the exact data schemas required for the BookstoreOnline application.

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         from datetime import datetime
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions for file operations and data parsing
         
         def read_file_lines(filename):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     return [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 return []
         
         def write_file_lines(filename, lines):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in lines:
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         # === Books ===
         def load_books():
             books = []
             lines = read_file_lines('books.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 8:
                     continue
                 try:
                     book = {
                         'book_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'title': parts[1],
                         'author': parts[2],
                         'isbn': parts[3],
                         'category': parts[4],
                         'price': float(parts[5]),
                         'stock': int(parts[6]),
                         'description': parts[7]
                     }
                     books.append(book)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return books
         
         def books_dict():
             books = load_books()
             return {b['book_id']: b for b in books}
         
         # === Categories ===
         def load_categories():
             categories = []
             lines = read_file_lines('categories.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 3:
                     continue
                 try:
                     category = {
                         'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'category_name': parts[1],
                         'description': parts[2]
                     }
                     categories.append(category)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return categories
         
         # === Cart ===
         def load_cart():
             cart = []
             lines = read_file_lines('cart.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 4:
                     continue
                 try:
                     item = {
                         'cart_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'book_id': int(parts[1]),
                         'quantity': int(parts[2]),
                         'added_date': parts[3]
                     }
                     cart.append(item)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return cart
         
         def save_cart(cart):
             lines = []
             for item in cart:
                 line = f"{item['cart_id']}|{item['book_id']}|{item['quantity']}|{item['added_date']}"
                 lines.append(line)
             write_file_lines('cart.txt', lines)
         
         # === Orders ===
         def load_orders():
             orders = []
             lines = read_file_lines('orders.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 6:
                     continue
                 try:
                     order = {
                         'order_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'customer_name': parts[1],
                         'order_date': parts[2],
                         'total_amount': float(parts[3]),
                         'status': parts[4],
                         'shipping_address': parts[5]
                     }
                     orders.append(order)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return orders
         
         # === Order Items ===
         def load_order_items():
             order_items = []
             lines = read_file_lines('order_items.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 5:
                     continue
                 try:
                     item = {
                         'order_item_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'order_id': int(parts[1]),
                         'book_id': int(parts[2]),
                         'quantity': int(parts[3]),
                         'price': float(parts[4])
                     }
                     order_items.append(item)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return order_items
         
         # === Reviews ===
         def load_reviews():
             reviews = []
             lines = read_file_lines('reviews.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 6:
                     continue
                 try:
                     review = {
                         'review_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'book_id': int(parts[1]),
                         'customer_name': parts[2],
                         'rating': int(parts[3]),
                         'review_text': parts[4],
                         'review_date': parts[5]
                     }
                     reviews.append(review)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return reviews
         
         # === Bestsellers ===
         def load_bestsellers():
             bestsellers = []
             lines = read_file_lines('bestsellers.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 3:
                     continue
                 try:
                     bestseller = {
                         'book_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'sales_count': int(parts[1]),
                         'period': parts[2]
                     }
                     bestsellers.append(bestseller)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return bestsellers
         
         # === Helpers ===
         def get_new_cart_id(cart):
             if not cart:
                 return 1
             return max(item['cart_id'] for item in cart) + 1
         
         def get_new_order_id(orders):
             if not orders:
                 return 1
             return max(order['order_id'] for order in orders) + 1
         
         def get_new_order_item_id(order_items):
             if not order_items:
                 return 1
             return max(item['order_item_id'] for item in order_items) + 1
         
         def get_new_review_id(reviews):
             if not reviews:
                 return 1
             return max(review['review_id'] for review in reviews) + 1
         
         # === Routes ===
         @app.route('/')
         def dashboard():
             books = load_books()
             featured_books = [{
                 'book_id': b['book_id'],
                 'title': b['title'],
                 'author': b['author'],
                 'price': b['price']
             } for b in books[:5]]
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_books=featured_books)
         
         
         @app.route('/catalog', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def book_catalog():
             books = load_books()
             categories = load_categories()
             selected_category = None
             search_query = ''
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Fix field names according to template
                 selected_category = request.form.get('selected_category')
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
         
             filtered_books = []
             for book in books:
                 include = True
                 if selected_category and selected_category != '':
                     # category filter expects category_name, match by name
                     if book['category'] != selected_category:
                         include = False
                 if search_query and search_query.lower() not in book['title'].lower() and search_query.lower() not in book['author'].lower():
                     include = False
                 if include:
                     filtered_books.append(book)
         
             books_for_template = [{
                 'book_id': b['book_id'],
                 'title': b['title'],
                 'author': b['author'],
                 'price': b['price']
             } for b in filtered_books]
         
             categories_for_template = [{
                 'category_id': str(c['category_id']),
                 'category_name': c['category_name']
             } for c in categories]
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', books=books_for_template, categories=categories_for_template, selected_category=selected_category if selected_category else None, search_query=search_query)
         
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def book_details(book_id):
             books = books_dict()
             book = books.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 return "Book not found", 404
         
             reviews_all = load_reviews()
             reviews_for_book = [r for r in reviews_all if r['book_id'] == book_id]
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if 'add-to-cart-button' in request.form:
                     cart = load_cart()
                     existing = next((item for item in cart if item['book_id'] == book_id), None)
                     if existing:
                         existing['quantity'] += 1
                     else:
                         new_cart_id = get_new_cart_id(cart)
                         today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                         cart.append({
                             'cart_id': new_cart_id,
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'quantity': 1,
                             'added_date': today
                         })
                     save_cart(cart)
                     return redirect(url_for('shopping_cart'))
         
             book_template = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'isbn': book['isbn'],
                 'category': book['category'],
                 'price': book['price'],
                 'stock': book['stock'],
                 'description': book['description']
             }
         
             return render_template('details.html', book=book_template, reviews=reviews_for_book)
         
         
         @app.route('/cart', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def shopping_cart():
             cart = load_cart()
             books = books_dict()
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Check removes by presence of button name 'remove-item'
                 remove_item_id = request.form.get('remove-item')
                 if remove_item_id:
                     try:
                         remove_item_id_int = int(remove_item_id)
                         cart = [item for item in cart if item['cart_id'] != remove_item_id_int]
                         save_cart(cart)
                         return redirect(url_for('shopping_cart'))
                     except Exception:
                         pass
         
                 updated = False
                 for item in cart[:]:
                     input_name = f'quantity-{item["cart_id"]}'
                     if input_name in request.form:
                         try:
                             new_qty = int(request.form[input_name])
                             if new_qty >= 0:
                                 if new_qty == 0:
                                     cart.remove(item)
                                 else:
                                     item['quantity'] = new_qty
                                 updated = True
                         except ValueError:
                             pass
                 if updated:
                     save_cart(cart)
                     return redirect(url_for('shopping_cart'))
         
             cart_items = []
             total_amount = 0.0
             for item in cart:
                 b = books.get(item['book_id'])
                 if b:
                     price = b['price']
                     quantity = item['quantity']
                     subtotal = price * quantity
                     total_amount += subtotal
                     cart_items.append({
                         'item_id': item['cart_id'],
                         'book_id': b['book_id'],
                         'title': b['title'],
                         'quantity': quantity,
                         'price': price,
                         'subtotal': subtotal
                     })
         
             return render_template('cart.html', cart_items=cart_items, total_amount=total_amount)
         
         
         @app.route('/checkout', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def checkout():
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if 'place-order-button' in request.form:
                     customer_name = request.form.get('customer_name', '').strip()
                     shipping_address = request.form.get('shipping_address', '').strip()
                     payment_method = request.form.get('payment_method', '').strip()
         
                     if not customer_name or not shipping_address or not payment_method:
                         return render_template('checkout.html')
         
                     cart = load_cart()
                     books = books_dict()
                     if not cart:
                         return render_template('checkout.html')
         
                     total_amount = 0.0
                     for item in cart:
                         b = books.get(item['book_id'])
                         if not b:
                             continue
                         total_amount += b['price'] * item['quantity']
         
                     orders = load_orders()
                     order_items = load_order_items()
         
                     new_order_id = get_new_order_id(orders)
                     today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
                     orders.append({
                         'order_id': new_order_id,
                         'customer_name': customer_name,
                         'order_date': today,
                         'total_amount': total_amount,
                         'status': 'Pending',
                         'shipping_address': shipping_address
                     })
         
                     next_order_item_id = get_new_order_item_id(order_items)
                     for item in cart:
                         b = books.get(item['book_id'])
                         if not b:
                             continue
                         order_items.append({
                             'order_item_id': next_order_item_id,
                             'order_id': new_order_id,
                             'book_id': b['book_id'],
                             'quantity': item['quantity'],
                             'price': b['price']
                         })
                         next_order_item_id += 1
         
                     order_lines = []
                     for o in orders:
                         line = f"{o['order_id']}|{o['customer_name']}|{o['order_date']}|{o['total_amount']:.2f}|{o['status']}|{o['shipping_address']}"
                         order_lines.append(line)
                     write_file_lines('orders.txt', order_lines)
         
                     order_items_lines = []
                     for oi in order_items:
                         line = f"{oi['order_item_id']}|{oi['order_id']}|{oi['book_id']}|{oi['quantity']}|{oi['price']:.2f}"
                         order_items_lines.append(line)
                     write_file_lines('order_items.txt', order_items_lines)
         
                     write_file_lines('cart.txt', [])
         
                     return redirect(url_for('order_history'))
         
             return render_template('checkout.html')
         
         
         @app.route('/orders', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def order_history():
             orders = load_orders()
             status_filter = 'All'
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Fix form field name from template
                 status_filter_input = request.form.get('status_filter')
                 if status_filter_input:
                     status_filter = status_filter_input
         
                 view_order_button = next((key for key in request.form.keys() if key.startswith('view-order-button-')), None)
                 if view_order_button:
                     # Since no view_order route, redirect back to history
                     return redirect(url_for('order_history'))
         
             if status_filter and status_filter != 'All':
                 orders_filtered = [o for o in orders if o['status'] == status_filter]
             else:
                 orders_filtered = orders
         
             return render_template('history.html', orders=orders_filtered, status_filter=status_filter)
         
         
         @app.route('/reviews', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def reviews():
             all_reviews = load_reviews()
             rating_filter = None
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if 'write-review-button' in request.form:
                     return redirect(url_for('write_review'))
         
                 # Fix field name from template
                 rating_selected = request.form.get('rating_filter')
                 if rating_selected:
                     try:
                         rating_val = int(rating_selected)
                         if 1 <= rating_val <= 5:
                             rating_filter = rating_val
                     except Exception:
                         pass
         
             if rating_filter:
                 filtered_reviews = [r for r in all_reviews if r['rating'] == rating_filter]
             else:
                 filtered_reviews = all_reviews
         
             return render_template('reviews.html', reviews=filtered_reviews, rating_filter=str(rating_filter) if rating_filter is not None else '')
         
         
         @app.route('/write_review', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def write_review():
             orders = load_orders()
             order_items = load_order_items()
             books = books_dict()
         
             purchased_book_ids = set()
             for oi in order_items:
                 purchased_book_ids.add(oi['book_id'])
         
             purchased_books = []
             for book_id in purchased_book_ids:
                 book = books.get(book_id)
                 if book:
                     purchased_books.append({
                         'book_id': book['book_id'],
                         'title': book['title']
                     })
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if 'submit-review-button' in request.form:
                     selected_book_id = request.form.get('select-book')
                     rating_select = request.form.get('rating-select')
                     review_text = request.form.get('review-text', '').strip()
         
                     try:
                         book_id_int = int(selected_book_id)
                         rating_int = int(rating_select)
                         if book_id_int not in purchased_book_ids or not (1 <= rating_int <= 5) or not review_text:
                             raise ValueError('Invalid input')
                     except Exception:
                         return render_template('write_review.html', purchased_books=purchased_books)
         
                     reviews_all = load_reviews()
                     new_review_id = get_new_review_id(reviews_all)
                     today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                     reviews_all.append({
                         'review_id': new_review_id,
                         'book_id': book_id_int,
                         'customer_name': 'Anonymous',
                         'rating': rating_int,
                         'review_text': review_text,
                         'review_date': today
                     })
         
                     review_lines = []
                     for r in reviews_all:
                         line = f"{r['review_id']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['customer_name']}|{r['rating']}|{r['review_text']}|{r['review_date']}"
                         review_lines.append(line)
                     write_file_lines('reviews.txt', review_lines)
         
                     return redirect(url_for('reviews'))
         
             return render_template('write_review.html', purchased_books=purchased_books)
         
         
         @app.route('/bestsellers', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def bestsellers():
             bestsellers_all = load_bestsellers()
             books = books_dict()
             time_period = 'All Time'
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Fix field name from template
                 time_period_filter = request.form.get('time_period')
                 if time_period_filter:
                     time_period = time_period_filter
         
                 view_book_button = next((key for key in request.form.keys() if key.startswith('view-book-button-')), None)
                 if view_book_button:
                     try:
                         book_id = int(view_book_button.split('-')[-1])
                         return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
                     except Exception:
                         pass
         
             filtered_bestsellers = [b for b in bestsellers_all if b['period'] == time_period]
             filtered_bestsellers.sort(key=lambda b: b['sales_count'], reverse=True)
         
             bestsellers_for_template = []
             for b in filtered_bestsellers:
                 book = books.get(b['book_id'])
                 if book:
                     bestsellers_for_template.append({
                         'book_id': book['book_id'],
                         'title': book['title'],
                         'author': book['author'],
                         'price': book['price'],
                         'sales_count': b['sales_count']
                     })
         
             return render_template('bestsellers.html', bestsellers=bestsellers_for_template, time_period=time_period)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         from datetime import datetime
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions for file operations and data parsing
         
         def read_file_lines(filename):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     return [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 return []
         
         def write_file_lines(filename, lines):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in lines:
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         # === Books ===
         def load_books():
             books = []
             lines = read_file_lines('books.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 8:
                     continue
                 try:
                     book = {
                         'book_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'title': parts[1],
                         'author': parts[2],
                         'isbn': parts[3],
                         'category': parts[4],
                         'price': float(parts[5]),
                         'stock': int(parts[6]),
                         'description': parts[7]
                     }
                     books.append(book)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return books
         
         def books_dict():
             books = load_books()
             return {b['book_id']: b for b in books}
         
         # === Categories ===
         def load_categories():
             categories = []
             lines = read_file_lines('categories.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 3:
                     continue
                 try:
                     category = {
                         'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'category_name': parts[1],
                         'description': parts[2]
                     }
                     categories.append(category)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return categories
         
         # === Cart ===
         def load_cart():
             cart = []
             lines = read_file_lines('cart.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 4:
                     continue
                 try:
                     item = {
                         'cart_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'book_id': int(parts[1]),
                         'quantity': int(parts[2]),
                         'added_date': parts[3]
                     }
                     cart.append(item)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return cart
         
         def save_cart(cart):
             lines = []
             for item in cart:
                 line = f"{item['cart_id']}|{item['book_id']}|{item['quantity']}|{item['added_date']}"
                 lines.append(line)
             write_file_lines('cart.txt', lines)
         
         # === Orders ===
         def load_orders():
             orders = []
             lines = read_file_lines('orders.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 6:
                     continue
                 try:
                     order = {
                         'order_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'customer_name': parts[1],
                         'order_date': parts[2],
                         'total_amount': float(parts[3]),
                         'status': parts[4],
                         'shipping_address': parts[5]
                     }
                     orders.append(order)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return orders
         
         # === Order Items ===
         def load_order_items():
             order_items = []
             lines = read_file_lines('order_items.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 5:
                     continue
                 try:
                     item = {
                         'order_item_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'order_id': int(parts[1]),
                         'book_id': int(parts[2]),
                         'quantity': int(parts[3]),
                         'price': float(parts[4])
                     }
                     order_items.append(item)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return order_items
         
         # === Reviews ===
         def load_reviews():
             reviews = []
             lines = read_file_lines('reviews.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 6:
                     continue
                 try:
                     review = {
                         'review_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'book_id': int(parts[1]),
                         'customer_name': parts[2],
                         'rating': int(parts[3]),
                         'review_text': parts[4],
                         'review_date': parts[5]
                     }
                     reviews.append(review)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return reviews
         
         # === Bestsellers ===
         def load_bestsellers():
             bestsellers = []
             lines = read_file_lines('bestsellers.txt')
             for line in lines:
                 parts = line.split('|')
                 if len(parts) != 3:
                     continue
                 try:
                     bestseller = {
                         'book_id': int(parts[0]),
                         'sales_count': int(parts[1]),
                         'period': parts[2]
                     }
                     bestsellers.append(bestseller)
                 except Exception:
                     continue
             return bestsellers
         
         # === Helpers ===
         def get_new_cart_id(cart):
             if not cart:
                 return 1
             return max(item['cart_id'] for item in cart) + 1
         
         def get_new_order_id(orders):
             if not orders:
                 return 1
             return max(order['order_id'] for order in orders) + 1
         
         def get_new_order_item_id(order_items):
             if not order_items:
                 return 1
             return max(item['order_item_id'] for item in order_items) + 1
         
         def get_new_review_id(reviews):
             if not reviews:
                 return 1
             return max(review['review_id'] for review in reviews) + 1
         
         # === Routes ===
         @app.route('/')
         def dashboard():
             books = load_books()
             featured_books = [{
                 'book_id': b['book_id'],
                 'title': b['title'],
                 'author': b['author'],
                 'price': b['price']
             } for b in books[:5]]
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_books=featured_books)
         
         
         @app.route('/catalog', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def book_catalog():
             books = load_books()
             categories = load_categories()
             selected_category = None
             search_query = ''
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Fix field names to match template
                 selected_category = request.form.get('selected_category')
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
         
             filtered_books = []
             for book in books:
                 include = True
                 if selected_category and selected_category != '':
                     if book['category'] != selected_category:
                         include = False
                 if search_query and search_query.lower() not in book['title'].lower() and search_query.lower() not in book['author'].lower():
                     include = False
                 if include:
                     filtered_books.append(book)
         
             books_for_template = [{
                 'book_id': b['book_id'],
                 'title': b['title'],
                 'author': b['author'],
                 'price': b['price']
             } for b in filtered_books]
         
             categories_for_template = [{
                 'category_id': str(c['category_id']),
                 'category_name': c['category_name']
             } for c in categories]
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', books=books_for_template, categories=categories_for_template, selected_category=selected_category if selected_category else None, search_query=search_query)
         
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def book_details(book_id):
             books = books_dict()
             book = books.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 return "Book not found", 404
         
             reviews_all = load_reviews()
             reviews_for_book = [r for r in reviews_all if r['book_id'] == book_id]
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if 'add-to-cart-button' in request.form:
                     cart = load_cart()
                     existing = next((item for item in cart if item['book_id'] == book_id), None)
                     if existing:
                         existing['quantity'] += 1
                     else:
                         new_cart_id = get_new_cart_id(cart)
                         today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                         cart.append({
                             'cart_id': new_cart_id,
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'quantity': 1,
                             'added_date': today
                         })
                     save_cart(cart)
                     return redirect(url_for('shopping_cart'))
         
             book_template = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'isbn': book['isbn'],
                 'category': book['category'],
                 'price': book['price'],
                 'stock': book['stock'],
                 'description': book['description']
             }
         
             return render_template('details.html', book=book_template, reviews=reviews_for_book)
         
         
         @app.route('/cart', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def shopping_cart():
             cart = load_cart()
             books = books_dict()
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 remove_item_id = request.form.get('remove-item')
                 if remove_item_id:
                     try:
                         remove_item_id_int = int(remove_item_id)
                         cart = [item for item in cart if item['cart_id'] != remove_item_id_int]
                         save_cart(cart)
                         return redirect(url_for('shopping_cart'))
                     except Exception:
                         pass
         
                 updated = False
                 for item in cart[:]:
                     input_name = f'quantity-{item["cart_id"]}'
                     if input_name in request.form:
                         try:
                             new_qty = int(request.form[input_name])
                             if new_qty >= 0:
                                 if new_qty == 0:
                                     cart.remove(item)
                                 else:
                                     item['quantity'] = new_qty
                                 updated = True
                         except ValueError:
                             pass
                 if updated:
                     save_cart(cart)
                     return redirect(url_for('shopping_cart'))
         
             cart_items = []
             total_amount = 0.0
             for item in cart:
                 b = books.get(item['book_id'])
                 if b:
                     price = b['price']
                     quantity = item['quantity']
                     subtotal = price * quantity
                     total_amount += subtotal
                     cart_items.append({
                         'item_id': item['cart_id'],
                         'book_id': b['book_id'],
                         'title': b['title'],
                         'quantity': quantity,
                         'price': price,
                         'subtotal': subtotal
                     })
         
             return render_template('cart.html', cart_items=cart_items, total_amount=total_amount)
         
         
         @app.route('/checkout', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def checkout():
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if 'place-order-button' in request.form:
                     customer_name = request.form.get('customer_name', '').strip()
                     shipping_address = request.form.get('shipping_address', '').strip()
                     payment_method = request.form.get('payment_method', '').strip()
         
                     if not customer_name or not shipping_address or not payment_method:
                         return render_template('checkout.html')
         
                     cart = load_cart()
                     books = books_dict()
                     if not cart:
                         return render_template('checkout.html')
         
                     total_amount = 0.0
                     for item in cart:
                         b = books.get(item['book_id'])
                         if not b:
                             continue
                         total_amount += b['price'] * item['quantity']
         
                     orders = load_orders()
                     order_items = load_order_items()
         
                     new_order_id = get_new_order_id(orders)
                     today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
                     orders.append({
                         'order_id': new_order_id,
                         'customer_name': customer_name,
                         'order_date': today,
                         'total_amount': total_amount,
                         'status': 'Pending',
                         'shipping_address': shipping_address
                     })
         
                     next_order_item_id = get_new_order_item_id(order_items)
                     for item in cart:
                         b = books.get(item['book_id'])
                         if not b:
                             continue
                         order_items.append({
                             'order_item_id': next_order_item_id,
                             'order_id': new_order_id,
                             'book_id': b['book_id'],
                             'quantity': item['quantity'],
                             'price': b['price']
                         })
                         next_order_item_id += 1
         
                     order_lines = []
                     for o in orders:
                         line = f"{o['order_id']}|{o['customer_name']}|{o['order_date']}|{o['total_amount']:.2f}|{o['status']}|{o['shipping_address']}"
                         order_lines.append(line)
                     write_file_lines('orders.txt', order_lines)
         
                     order_items_lines = []
                     for oi in order_items:
                         line = f"{oi['order_item_id']}|{oi['order_id']}|{oi['book_id']}|{oi['quantity']}|{oi['price']:.2f}"
                         order_items_lines.append(line)
                     write_file_lines('order_items.txt', order_items_lines)
         
                     write_file_lines('cart.txt', [])
         
                     return redirect(url_for('order_history'))
         
             return render_template('checkout.html')
         
         
         @app.route('/orders', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def order_history():
             orders = load_orders()
             status_filter = 'All'
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Fix name to match template
                 status_filter_selected = request.form.get('status_filter')
                 if status_filter_selected:
                     status_filter = status_filter_selected
         
                 view_order_button = next((key for key in request.form.keys() if key.startswith('view-order-button-')), None)
                 if view_order_button:
                     # No view_order route, so disable function
                     pass
         
             if status_filter and status_filter != 'All':
                 orders_filtered = [o for o in orders if o['status'] == status_filter]
             else:
                 orders_filtered = orders
         
             return render_template('history.html', orders=orders_filtered, status_filter=status_filter)
         
         
         @app.route('/reviews', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def reviews():
             all_reviews = load_reviews()
             rating_filter = None
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if 'write-review-button' in request.form:
                     return redirect(url_for('write_review'))
         
                 # Fix name to match template
                 rating_selected = request.form.get('rating_filter')
                 if rating_selected:
                     try:
                         rating_val = int(rating_selected)
                         if 1 <= rating_val <= 5:
                             rating_filter = rating_val
                     except Exception:
                         pass
         
             if rating_filter:
                 filtered_reviews = [r for r in all_reviews if r['rating'] == rating_filter]
             else:
                 filtered_reviews = all_reviews
         
             return render_template('reviews.html', reviews=filtered_reviews, rating_filter=str(rating_filter) if rating_filter is not None else '')
         
         
         @app.route('/write_review', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def write_review():
             orders = load_orders()
             order_items = load_order_items()
             books = books_dict()
         
             purchased_book_ids = set()
             for oi in order_items:
                 purchased_book_ids.add(oi['book_id'])
         
             purchased_books = []
             for book_id in purchased_book_ids:
                 book = books.get(book_id)
                 if book:
                     purchased_books.append({
                         'book_id': book['book_id'],
                         'title': book['title']
                     })
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if 'submit-review-button' in request.form:
                     selected_book_id = request.form.get('select-book')
                     rating_select = request.form.get('rating-select')
                     review_text = request.form.get('review-text', '').strip()
         
                     try:
                         book_id_int = int(selected_book_id)
                         rating_int = int(rating_select)
                         if book_id_int not in purchased_book_ids or not (1 <= rating_int <= 5) or not review_text:
                             raise ValueError('Invalid input')
                     except Exception:
                         return render_template('write_review.html', purchased_books=purchased_books)
         
                     reviews_all = load_reviews()
                     new_review_id = get_new_review_id(reviews_all)
                     today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                     reviews_all.append({
                         'review_id': new_review_id,
                         'book_id': book_id_int,
                         'customer_name': 'Anonymous',
                         'rating': rating_int,
                         'review_text': review_text,
                         'review_date': today
                     })
         
                     review_lines = []
                     for r in reviews_all:
                         line = f"{r['review_id']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['customer_name']}|{r['rating']}|{r['review_text']}|{r['review_date']}"
                         review_lines.append(line)
                     write_file_lines('reviews.txt', review_lines)
         
                     return redirect(url_for('reviews'))
         
             return render_template('write_review.html', purchased_books=purchased_books)
         
         
         @app.route('/bestsellers', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def bestsellers():
             bestsellers_all = load_bestsellers()
             books = books_dict()
             time_period = 'All Time'
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Fix name to match template
                 time_period_filter = request.form.get('time_period')
                 if time_period_filter:
                     time_period = time_period_filter
         
                 view_book_button = next((key for key in request.form.keys() if key.startswith('view-book-button-')), None)
                 if view_book_button:
                     try:
                         book_id = int(view_book_button.split('-')[-1])
                         return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
                     except Exception:
                         pass
         
             filtered_bestsellers = [b for b in bestsellers_all if b['period'] == time_period]
             filtered_bestsellers.sort(key=lambda b: b['sales_count'], reverse=True)
         
             bestsellers_for_template = []
             for b in filtered_bestsellers:
                 book = books.get(b['book_id'])
                 if book:
                     bestsellers_for_template.append({
                         'book_id': book['book_id'],
                         'title': book['title'],
                         'author': book['author'],
                         'price': book['price'],
                         'sales_count': b['sales_count']
                     })
         
             return render_template('bestsellers.html', bestsellers=bestsellers_for_template, time_period=time_period)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)
